The bug occurs when the code doesn't account\nfor this rename and still uses the old key name for Qt 6.4, causing Chromium\nto ignore the setting.\n\nThis test verifies that:\n- On Qt 6.4, the threshold.text setting produces the correct Chromium key\n  name (ForegroundBrightnessThreshold, not TextBrightnessThreshold)\n- The setting appears in the dark-mode-settings switch\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport os\n\n# Set Qt to use offscreen platform before any Qt imports\nos.environ['QT_QPA_PLATFORM'] = 'offscreen'\n\n# Add the qutebrowser directory to the path\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\n\nimport pytest\n\n\ndef test_qt64_text_threshold_setting_uses_correct_chromium_key(monkeypatch):\n    \"\"\"Test that Qt 6.4 uses ForegroundBrightnessThreshold for text threshold.\n\n    This is a regression test for issue #7904 where the text brightness threshold\n    setting has no effect on Qt 6.4 because the Chromium setting key was renamed\n    from TextBrightnessThreshold to ForegroundBrightnessThreshold.\n\n    FAILS on buggy code: The test will fail because the code still uses\n    'TextBrightnessThreshold' for Qt 6.4 instead of 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'.\n\n    PASSES on fixed code: After the fix, the test passes because Qt 6.4 correctly\n    uses 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'.\n    \"\"\"\n    from qutebrowser.utils import usertypes, version\n    from qutebrowser.browser.webengine import darkmode\n    from qutebrowser.misc import objects\n    from qutebrowser.config import config as config_module\n\n    # Setup backend\n    monkeypatch.setattr(objects, 'backend', usertypes.Backend.QtWebEngine)\n\n    # Create a simple config stub\n    class ConfigStub:\n        def get(self, name, fallback=False):\n            if name == 'colors.webpage.preferred_color_scheme':\n                return usertypes.UNSET\n            if name == 'colors.webpage.darkmode.enabled':\n                return True\n            if name == 'colors.webpage.darkmode.algorithm':\n                return 'brightness-rgb'\n            if name == 'colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text':\n                return 100\n            if name == 'colors.webpage.darkmode.policy.images':\n                return 'smart'\n            return fallback\n\n    class ConfigVal:\n        def __init__(self):\n            self.colors = ColorsConfig()\n\n    class ColorsConfig:\n        def __init__(self):\n            self.webpage = WebpageConfig()\n\n    class WebpageConfig:\n        def __init__(self):\n            self.darkmode = DarkmodeConfig()\n            self.preferred_color_scheme = usertypes.UNSET\n\n    class DarkmodeConfig:\n        enabled = True\n        algorithm = 'brightness-rgb'\n        threshold = ThresholdConfig()\n        policy = PolicyConfig()\n\n    class ThresholdConfig:\n        text = 100\n        background = usertypes.UNSET\n\n    class PolicyConfig:\n        images = 'smart'\n        page = usertypes.UNSET\n\n    config_stub = ConfigStub()\n    config_val = ConfigVal()\n\n    monkeypatch.setattr(config_module, 'instance', config_stub)\n    monkeypatch.setattr(config_module, 'val', config_val)\n\n    # Create versions object for Qt 6.4\n    versions = version.WebEngineVersions.from_pyqt('6.4.0')\n\n    # Get the dark mode settings\n    settings = darkmode.settings(versions=versions, special_flags=[])\n\n    # Verify the structure:\n    # On Qt 6.4, settings should be in two switches: blink-settings and dark-mode-settings\n    assert 'dark-mode-settings' in settings, \\\n        f\"Dark mode settings should be in 'dark-mode-settings' switch for Qt 6.4. Got: {settings}\"\n\n    dark_mode_settings = settings['dark-mode-settings']\n\n    # Find the threshold setting in the output\n    threshold_setting = None\n    for key, value in dark_mode_settings:\n        if key in ('TextBrightnessThreshold', 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'):\n            threshold_setting = (key, value)\n            break\n\n    # The test assertion that will fail on buggy code\n    assert threshold_setting is not None, \\\n        (f\"Threshold setting should be present in dark mode settings. \"\n         f\"Got settings: {dark_mode_settings}\")\n\n    key, value = threshold_setting\n\n    # BUG CHECK: On buggy code, this will be 'TextBrightnessThreshold'\n    # On fixed code, this will be 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'\n    assert key == 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold', \\\n        (f\"Qt 6.4 should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (Chromium renamed the setting), \"\n         f\"but got '{key}'. This indicates the bug where the text threshold setting \"\n         f\"has no effect on Qt 6.4 because Chromium expects the new key name. \"\n         f\"Full settings: {dark_mode_settings}\")\n\n    assert value == '100', \\\n        f\"Threshold value should be '100', but got '{value}'\"\n\n\ndef test_qt63_text_threshold_setting_uses_old_chromium_key(monkeypatch):\n    \"\"\"Test that Qt 6.3 still uses TextBrightnessThreshold.\n\n    Qt 6.3 was released before Chromium made the rename, so it should still\n    use the old TextBrightnessThreshold key.\n    \"\"\"\n    from qutebrowser.utils import usertypes, version\n    from qutebrowser.browser.webengine import darkmode\n    from qutebrowser.misc import objects\n    from qutebrowser.config import config as config_module\n\n    #
